# 1 ANALYSES POUR: le chasseur offrait un coyote a nicole
# Analyse 1 sur 1
(P[]
  (GN[acc=[gr='m', nb='sg']]
    (Det[acc=[gr='m', nb='sg'], det='+'] le)
    (N[acc=[gr='m', nb='sg']] chasseur))
  (GV[acc=[nb='sg', pers=3, tens='pst']]
    (VD[acc=[nb='sg', pers=3, tens='pst']] offrait)
    (GN[acc=[gr='m', nb='sg']]
      (Det[acc=[gr='m', nb='sg'], det='+'] un)
      (N[acc=[gr='m', nb='sg']] coyote))
    (GP[]
      (Prep[det='+'] a)
      (GN[acc=[gr='f', nb='sg']] (Npr[acc=[gr='f', nb='sg']] nicole)))))
